tests pass `lambda: _FIXED_NOW`); freezegun explicitly REJECTED — not transitive in pytest-asyncio set, asyncio-flakier than callable injection; D5 dep-footprint per §0.9 — `apscheduler==3.10.4` runtime dep added to `services/execution/pyproject.toml` only (not workspace-level); - [x] T-F2+: ADR-Q-B — cumulative-delta P&L reconciliation strategy ADR (2026-05-02) — `docs/adr/0006-cumulative-delta-reconciliation-strategy.md` (168 LOC). Locks 5 operational decisions D1-D5 + D6 hazard-test mapping for §9.5:1592-1599 cumulative-delta close flow that brief leaves open: D1 snapshot pair triggers ONLY on full-close (`ps_after.remaining_qty == Decimal("0")` post-fill matching T-218b dispatcher boundary; partial-TP fills do NOT trigger snapshot pairs — cumulative semantics absorb partial-TP rows into final-close delta); D2 `Settings.execution_closed_pnl_post_close_sleep_s: float = 2.0` (range 0.0-30.0 per §N9; single sleep BEFORE the AFTER snapshot only — BEFORE is baseline read with no Bybit lag race per H-011); D3 single-trade single-call attribution (full delta to trigger trade; serializes naturally per-bot via T-218b's single asyncio.Task + per-sub-account Lock per D4 for cross-bot); D4 per-sub-account `asyncio.Lock` keyed on `sub_account` string (NOT bot_id — per ADR-0004 multiple bots may share sub_account; lifespan creates `closed_pnl_locks: dict[str, asyncio.Lock]`; F2 single-process scope per §3.1; F5+ sharding revisit replaces with NATS KV CAS / PG advisory lock); D5 atomic close persistence inside caller's tx (`update_trade_close(trade_id, realized_pnl=delta, fees_paid, close_reason, exit_price, closed_at, close_order_id)` per H-018 PK-only + `delete_position_state(bot_id, symbol)` composite-PK + post-commit `OrderClosed` emit per Q2 publish-after-persist; close_reason derives from exec_type — 'close'→'manual', 'sl'/'trail'→same, 'unknown'→'unknown' operator-actionable; close_order_id synthetic-fill resolution via T-218b's `select_open_order_id_by_trade_id` for trail/SL fills bez `executions.order_id` match — anchor to entry order context per FK NOT NULL invariant). auth ack / pong / subscribe-ack frames silently skipped (no topic). **H-009 no-dedup at adapter**: `test_duplicate_execId_frames_both_appear_in_executions_iterator` pins that adapter emits raw events including duplicates — T-218 dispatcher dedups via `DedupingConsumer` ring 10k. **Auth failure handling**: `success:false` → `auth_failure_count += 1` + ERROR log + reconnect loop continues (transport-level reconnect does NOT increment counter — pinned by `test_transport_reconnect_does_not_increment_auth_failure_count` per Write-time guidance #7). **Heartbeat**: app-level `{op:"ping"}` JSON frame every 18s + native `ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=10` transport-level backstop (Bybit V5 expects JSON ping; native PING control may not satisfy server idle window). **AsyncIterator factories**: `def executions(self) -> AsyncIterator[ExecutionEvent]: return self._iter_executions()` (`def` NOT `async def` per T-201 OQ-1, mirror `PaperExchange.stream_executions` shape); `_iter_executions` is async generator yielding from unbounded `asyncio.Queue.get()` (unbounded per OQ-2 default A — bounded + drop violates H-009 silent-loss; PaperExchange's bounded queue acceptable in-process, live WS not). **§N9 evaluation**: ctor kwargs `ws_url`, `ping_interval_s`, `long_disconnect_threshold_s` operator-tunable; module constants `_BACKOFF_BASE_S=1.0`, `_BACKOFF_CAP_S=60.0`, `_AUTH_PAYLOAD_PREFIX="GET/realtime"`, `_AUTH_EXPIRES_OFFSET_S=5` are Bybit-spec literals NOT operationally tunable per L-001 active control (mirror T-207 `_RECV_WINDOW_MS=5000` precedent). **Mappers**: `_map_execution_event` reads `execId/orderId/symbol/side/execPrice/execQty/execFee/execTime` from Bybit V5 wire → ExecutionEvent with `Decimal(str(...))` round-trip + UTC `executed_at` via `datetime.fromtimestamp(int(execTime)/1000, tz=UTC)`; `_map_position_event` mirrors T-208b `_map_position_row` field-for-field + `occurred_at` from `updatedTime` (duplication, not shared `PositionMapper` class — surface-expansion guard per OQ-9 default A). **L-006 LOC monitoring**: plan estimate 220 src; actual ws.py ~340 (raw incl docstrings), substantive ~289; production diff total ~358 LOC under §0.3 cap of 400. T-207 deltas: `packages/exchange/pyproject.toml` (+1 LOC `httpx==0.28.1` dep declaration matching `packages/market` version pin per OQ-1 default A — no new ecosystem dep) + new subpackage. **BybitV5Client surface**: 5-kwarg ctor (`api_key`, `api_secret`, `base_url="https://api.bybit.com"`, `connect_timeout=5.0`, `read_timeout=10.0`); `request(method, path, *, params, body, retries: int)` returns Bybit envelope `result` field on `retCode==0` or raises typed exception per §11.3. State-free across calls — signing per-call; `httpx.AsyncClient` owns connection pool. T-208 will extend ctor with adapter-level wrapping (`limiter`, `bus`, `sub_account`). `__aenter__/__aexit__/close()` lifecycle mirror `BinanceRestClient` (T-101 precedent). **HMAC-SHA256 signing** per Bybit V5 spec: payload `f"{timestamp_ms}{api_key}{recv_window}{query_or_body}"`; `signature = hmac.new(api_secret.encode("utf-8"), payload.encode("utf-8"), hashlib.sha256).hexdigest()`; 4 X-BAPI-* headers (`X-BAPI-API-KEY`, `X-BAPI-TIMESTAMP`, `X-BAPI-RECV-WINDOW=5000ms`, `X-BAPI-SIGN`). Stdlib `hmac` + `hashlib` only — no new third-party dep. **Retry matrix** per §11.2 verbatim: `max_attempts = retries + 1` loop; on `httpx.ConnectError`/`ReadTimeout`/`PoolTimeout` OR HTTP 5xx → if attempts remain, sleep `_backoff_delay(attempt)` then retry, else raise `NetworkTimeout`; on HTTP 401/403 → `AuthError` (no retry); on HTTP 429 → `RateLimitError` (no retry — caller's job to back off via shared pause flag); on HTTP 200 → parse Bybit envelope, on `JSONDecodeError` raise `ExchangeError` with `__cause__`, on `retCode==0` return `result` field, else `_translate_retcode(retcode, retmsg)`. **`_translate_retcode`** static method: `_RETCODE_RATE_LIMIT={10006, 10016}`→`RateLimitError`, `_RETCODE_AUTH={10003, 10004}`→`AuthError`, `_RETCODE_REJECT={10001, 10005}`→`OrderRejected(reason=retmsg)`, other non-zero→generic `ExchangeError`. **Jitter formula** per §F.3: `_backoff_delay(attempt) = _BASE_BACKOFF_S[min(attempt, len-1)] * (1.0 + random.uniform(-_JITTER_PCT, _JITTER_PCT))` with `_BASE_BACKOFF_S=(0.5, 1.0, 2.0)` + `_JITTER_PCT=0.1` ±10%; clamp at last entry for attempts≥3. `# noqa: S311 # nosec B311` annotation explicitly justifies operational-jitter-not-cryptographic use (distinct from cryptographic `hashlib.sha256`). **W#1 sort canonicalization fix applied**: `_sign_request` calls `urlencode(sorted(params.items()))` AND `_send` calls `dict(sorted(params.items()))` — single load-bearing invariant in BOTH paths so Bybit doesn't reject with sign mismatch when Python dict insertion order differs from alphabetical. **W#2 body parity fix applied**: `_send` pre-serializes body once via `json.dumps(body, separators=(",", ":")).encode("utf-8")` and passes via `content=` kwarg (NOT `json=` which may re-serialize differently); identical compact JSON used in `_sign_request` payload tail. **§N3 markers correctly NOT on T-207 internals** per Decision #9: `_request_with_retry`, `_sign_request`, `_translate_retcode`, `_backoff_delay`, `request` are LOW-LEVEL HTTP helpers; markers belong on T-208 method wrappers (`place_market_order @non_idempotent`, etc.) which are the actual `ExchangeClient` Protocol surface (T-201 already has them on the Protocol). **§N6 globals**: `BybitV5Client` per-instance state; module-level constants (`_RECV_WINDOW_MS=5000`, `_BASE_BACKOFF_S`, `_JITTER_PCT=0.1`, frozensets, `logger`) protocol-binding read-only per §11.2 verbatim — mirror T-205 `_MAX_CAS_RETRIES=3` / ADR-0003 §3 baked-in precedent. **§N9 configurability**: protocol-binding constants are NOT operational tunables; baked-in per Bybit V5 docs. **§N1 UTC**: timestamp via `time.time_ns() // 1_000_000` (UTC ms epoch per Bybit V5 spec). **§N7 thin adapter**: REST envelope at I/O boundary; no business logic. **H-003 zero-retry binding**: `_request_with_retry` with `retries=0` → `max_attempts=1` → single attempt → on `httpx.ReadTimeout`/etc. raise `NetworkTimeout` immediate (no sleep, no retry). T-208 `place_market_order` will pass `retries=0` per §11.2 + catch `NetworkTimeout` + raise `UnknownState(last_known_action="place_market_order")` per §11.3 H-003 binding (decoupled per OQ-8 default A). Test pin `test_request_with_retry_zero_retries_raises_immediately_on_timeout` asserts `mock_request.await_count == 1` AND `captured_sleeps == []`. **H-022 per-bot credentials**: ctor takes `api_key`/`api_secret` as plain kwargs; T-215 reads from env per-bot via `BOT_<ID>_BYBIT_API_KEY/SECRET` pattern (out of T-207 scope, correctly delegated). Subclass binds `key_fn: Callable[[T], str]` at construction; capacity defaults to 10000 per H-009 + §9.5 line 1591 verbatim ("ring buffer, size 10k"); raises `ValueError` if `capacity <= 0`. **Distinct mechanism, NOT JetStream `Nats-Msg-Id`/`duplicate_window`** (publisher-side, server-managed) and **NOT signal-gateway `DedupRing`** (TTL-based vs T-210 size-bounded). Two layers can coexist; address different replay sources. Module docstring contrasts both explicitly. **Locking invariant load-bearing** (W#1): `asyncio.Lock` protects ring (keys-seen tracking), NOT handler — `_process` runs OUTSIDE the locked section so a slow handler does not block ring updates. Subclasses must be re-entrancy-safe at the `_process` level if concurrent handler invocation matters across distinct keys. Eviction: `OrderedDict.popitem(last=False)` FIFO when `len > capacity` (W#3 `>` not `>=`; ring stays at exactly `capacity` entries in stable state, verified by `test_ring_stays_at_capacity_under_overflow`). Mirrors T-100 lifespan ordering convention (numbered-step docstring + reverse-shutdown). **Lifespan order (load-bearing per `docs/plans/T-110d.md` §"Hand verification"):** (1) `features_by_key = build_features()`; (2) `capacity_map = {key: max(feature.warmup_candles for _, feature in entries)}`; (3) `BufferRegistry(capacity_map)`; (4) `pool = create_pool(..., init=_register_jsonb_codec)` (T-110b Hand-off option (a)); (5) `bus = NatsClient(...); bus.connect()`; (6) `pipeline = FeaturePipeline(...)`; (7) `pipeline.acquire_handles()` (sync — allocates buffers); (8) `await warmup_load(..., source=SOURCE_BINANCE)` (pushes cagg history into now-allocated buffers in time order); (9) `await pipeline.start_consuming()` (subscribes to `market.ohlc.1m.>`); (10) state attach pool/bus/buffer_registry/pipeline → app.state. **Reverse shutdown:** `pipeline.stop()` BEFORE `bus.close()` BEFORE `pool.close()`. **Q11 race resolution** (Decision #11) — split T-110c's monolithic `pipeline.start()` into `acquire_handles()` (sync) + `start_consuming()` (async). Without the split: warmup-pre-start would silent-drop on un-allocated buffers (T-110a Decision #2 silent no-op on push to no-handles key); warmup-post-start would race live NATS frames and wedge out-of-order data into the deque (`Feature.compute` would see wedged candles → wrong output). The `acquire → warmup → subscribe` sequence closes both races. ~15 LOC patch to T-110c `pipeline.py` + 1 test split in `test_pipeline.py` (`test_start_acquires_handles_then_subscribes` → `test_acquire_handles_creates_handle_per_key` (sync, NO `@pytest.mark.asyncio`) + `test_start_consuming_subscribes_market_ohlc_1m` (async)). **JSONB codec via `packages/db/pool.py:create_pool` `init` callback extension** (T-110b Hand-off option (a)) — `_register_jsonb_codec` module-level helper in `main.py` registers `json.dumps`/`json.loads` per-connection so production `insert_feature(value_json=...)` writes round-trip dict ↔ JSONB without per-call codec registration; `test_register_jsonb_codec_calls_set_type_codec` verifies callback contract at unit level (mocks Connection, asserts `set_type_codec("jsonb", encoder=json.dumps, decoder=json.loads, schema="pg_catalog")` verbatim per Write-time guidance #3). asyncpg-stubs declares positional-only Protocol `_InitCallback` that doesn't structurally match `Callable[[Connection[Record]], Awaitable[None]]`; `init=init` pass-through carries `# type: ignore[arg-type]` with inline 3-line WHY rationale (live error code per `feedback_type_ignore_context` memory). **`SOURCE_BINANCE` single-source-of-truth** via new `services/feature_engine/app/constants.py: Final = "binance"` (Write-time guidance #2). **Decision #14 deviation from plan** (defensible improvement): T-110c shipped `pipeline.py` with `_SOURCE_BINANCE = "binance"` DECLARED-BUT-UNUSED (no callsite — `_wire_to_domain` uses `payload.source` from the wire payload). - [x] T-110a: feature-engine rolling candle buffer registry — refcounted, H-014 (2026-04-26) — first half of T-110 preemptive split (L-007 — original T-110 estimated ~350 LOC integration-heavy with five distinct concerns; pure-domain buffer abstraction extracted to its own task ahead of mid-write split). **`packages/features/buffers/registry.py`** ships `BufferRegistry` + `BufferHandle` with refcount lifecycle: one `collections.deque` per `(symbol, interval)` key sized to capacity declared at registry construction, lazy-allocated on the 0→1 acquire transition and deallocated on the 1→0 release transition. `acquire(symbol, interval) -> BufferHandle` raises `KeyError` for keys absent from `capacity_map`; `push(symbol, interval, candle)` is a silent no-op on unknown / zero-refcount keys (defensive against T-110b NATS handler routing candles for not-yet-acquired symbols during warmup ordering — both conditions reduce to "no entry in `_buffers`" so the lookup is the single guard). `BufferHandle` is a sync `AbstractContextManager`; `tail(n) -> tuple[OhlcCandle, ...]` returns an immutable snapshot via `tuple(itertools.islice(buffer, max(0, len-n), len))` — shorter tuple on under-fill (Feature implementations raise `FeatureUnderflowError` on insufficient warmup; registry is dumb storage). Single `_released: bool` flag on the handle short-circuits both `tail()` (raises `RuntimeError`) and double-`__exit__` (idempotent no-op); no per-handle counter. **H-014 contract** — multiple features that consume the same `(symbol, interval)` (EMA-20 + EMA-50 + RSI-14 over `("BTCUSDT", "15m")`) hold individual handles on the same shared deque; when one feature releases (T-111 plugin reload or shutdown order), the buffer must remain alive for the others. `test_refcount_buffer_survives_one_holder_releasing` mirrors `test_refcount_sub_survives_one_caller_releasing` (T-101c `packages/market/subscription.py`) verbatim, walking trace steps 1-9 of the plan's hand-verification table. **§N7 hexagonal** — buffers/ imports only stdlib (`itertools`, `collections.deque`, `contextlib.AbstractContextManager`, `typing.Self`, `typing.TYPE_CHECKING`) plus `packages.features.types.OhlcCandle` under TYPE_CHECKING. Zero `packages.bus`/`packages.db`/`asyncio`/`nats`/`asyncpg` hits — verified by `rg "^(import|from)" packages/features/buffers/` grep guard. Sync API; T-110b's single-threaded asyncio event loop serialises access. `packages/features/__init__.py` deliberately NOT touched — buffers are a T-110b composition-root dep imported via explicit `from packages.features.buffers import …`, keeping the public feature API surface narrow. **Tests** (15 new, 219 LOC): `test_buffers_registry.py` covers acquire-creates-buffer / acquire-unknown-raises / two-acquires-share-buffer / different-keys-isolated / H-014-survives-one-holder-releasing / release-to-zero-deallocates / push-no-holders-silent-drop / push-unknown-key-silent-drop / tail-immutable-snapshot / tail-underfill / tail-empty / tail-after-release-raises / double-release-idempotent / capacity-overflow-drops-oldest / acquire-after-dealloc-fresh-buffer (behavioural divergence test per Write-time guidance #3, NOT `is` identity — push-then-tail asserts prior data is gone). **Cap-relevant LOC**: `__init__.py` 13 + `registry.py` 198 = **211 source LOC, under §0.3 cap of 400** (plan estimated ~145; +46% docstring overhead on a small logical surface ~80 executable LOC; consistent with L-006 lesson). - [x] T-108: migration 0004 — `features` hypertable per §7.2 + §18.3 (2026-04-26) — closes §7.2 lines 900-915 + §18.3 lines 1174 + 1182-1183 by landing the storage layer for the §8.4 `FeatureUpdate` schema. Unblocks T-110 (feature-engine persist via §9.3 line 1494 ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE) and T-112 (backfill_features upsert). **`migrations/versions/0004_features_hypertable.py`** ships verbatim §7.2 DDL: 7 columns (`feature_name TEXT NOT NULL`, `symbol TEXT NOT NULL` denormalized, `computed_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL` hypertable time column, `value_num DOUBLE PRECISION` nullable, `value_bool BOOLEAN` nullable, `value_json JSONB` nullable, `source_version TEXT NOT NULL`), composite PK `(feature_name, symbol, computed_at, source_version)` exact-matching the §9.3 line 1494 ON CONFLICT target, hypertable with 7-day `chunk_time_interval`, secondary btree index `features_latest (feature_name, symbol, computed_at DESC)` per §7.2 line 914 verbatim. **`value_num` is `sa.Double()`** (compiles to PG `DOUBLE PRECISION` = 8 bytes / 53-bit mantissa) per §7.2 line 907 verbatim — `sa.Float()` would silently downgrade to PG `real` (4 bytes / 24-bit mantissa) and trip the test_0004 column-shape assertion. plan-reviewer caught this as BLOCKER in the first review round. **§18.3 lifecycle**: 30-day compression policy with `compress_segmentby = 'feature_name, symbol'` (matches the natural per-feature time-range scan pattern used by warmup, scoring snapshots, analytics drilldown) + `compress_orderby = 'computed_at DESC'` (mirrors T-103 precedent for `ohlc_1m`; brief §18.3 line 1182 specifies only segmentby, orderby is opt-in optimisation matching the latest-first query pattern); 180-day retention policy. **`value_*` columns nullable at DB layer** is a deliberate divergence from app-layer "exactly one non-None" — `FeatureValue.__post_init__` (T-106) enforces the invariant in code; T-110 is the only writer and is pre-validated through FeatureValue. **No DB-side CHECK constraint** on `(value_num IS NOT NULL)::int + (value_bool IS NOT NULL)::int + (value_json IS NOT NULL)::int = 1` — would add per-row write overhead without new protection beyond the app-layer guard. **No GIN index on `value_json`** — F1 queries (T-110 dispatch + scoring-engine KV reads) go through the composite PK / `features_latest` btree; brief §7.2 line 914 specifies only `features_latest`. F1+ entry queued for analytics-driven JSONB extraction in F4+ if observed. **Symmetric-stub downgrade per §N8 forward-only**: drops policies (with `if_exists => true`) before `op.drop_table("features")` (cascade-drops the hypertable's chunks per the T-103/0003 precedent — `DROP TABLE` removes the hypertable entry and all chunks; TimescaleDB metadata is cleaned up automatically). **Tests** (1 integration test, 231 LOC, env-gated `POSTGRES_TEST_DSN` per existing migrations conftest): mirrors test_0003 introspection patterns. Verifies (1) column shape via `information_schema.columns ORDER BY ordinal_position` with explicit `_EXPECTED_FEATURES_COLUMNS` tuple (`("value_num", "double precision", "YES")` is the post-hoc gate against the `sa.Double()` storage type decision); (2) composite PK ordinal `(feature_name, symbol, computed_at, source_version)` via `information_schema.table_constraints` JOIN `key_column_usage`; (3) hypertable + 7-day chunk_time_interval via `timescaledb_information.dimensions`; (4) compression `segmentby = ['feature_name', 'symbol']` + `orderby = [('computed_at', False, True)]` (DESC + nulls-first) via `timescaledb_information.compression_settings`; (5) retention + compression bgw_job entries via `_timescaledb_config.bgw_job` proc_name lookup with hypertable resolution through `_timescaledb_catalog.hypertable.table_name = 'features'` (simpler than test_0003 because no continuous aggregate to disambiguate via COALESCE); (6) `features_latest` btree shape via `pg_indexes.indexdef` substring match on `(feature_name, symbol, computed_at DESC)`; (7) end-to-end smoke — 3 INSERTs, one per `value_*` variant (float `70.5`, bool `True`, JSONB `{"upper": 50100.5, "middle": 50000.0, "lower": 49899.5}`) — round-trip via PK with explicit asyncpg JSONB codec `set_type_codec("jsonb", encoder=json.dumps, decoder=json.loads, schema="pg_catalog")` registered before SELECT (asyncpg defaults to raw JSON string; per-connection codec is the right scope, no global codec exists in conftests). plan-reviewer caught the codec requirement as CONCERN in the first review round; (8) `alembic_version = "0004"`. **Cap-relevant LOC**: migration 131 source + test 231 = 362; migrations also qualify under §0.3 generated-artifacts exception per T-100/T-103 precedent. - [x] T-107b: VWAP + Bollinger + MACD built-in indicators + `_sma_seeded_ema_series` helper (2026-04-26) — completes the §9.3 line 1488 six-indicator scope sketched in T-107a's preemptive split. SMA/OI change/funding rate listed in §9.3 remain F1+ (no current consumer). §N4 TDD-for-financial-math active per indicator with hand-computable deterministic fixtures. **`packages/features/builtins/vwap.py`** — `VwapFeature(session="daily", interval="1m")` with cumulative session VWAP: `typical_i = (high_i + low_i + close_i) / 3`, `VWAP = sum(typical_i * volume_i) / sum(volume_i)` over candles within the latest UTC date. Engine (T-110) supplies an arbitrarily-wide window; indicator filters to candles whose `bucket_start.date()` matches the latest candle's UTC date (single session); older candles silently dropped. **Zero-volume edge** raises `FeatureUnderflowError` per §0.4 fail-loud (degenerate input class — VWAP undefined when total_volume=0). `name_template = "ind.{symbol}.{interval}.vwap_session"` matches §B.2 line 3079 verbatim — session enum stays as constructor parameter for forward-compat with F1+ hourly/weekly but is NOT part of the identifier; T-111 registry will carry `params: {session: daily}` alongside the name in the YAML config. Constructor rejects `session != "daily"` (F1+ sessions deferred). `warmup_candles = 1`. **`packages/features/builtins/bollinger.py`** — `BollingerFeature(period=20, std_dev_multiplier=Decimal("2"), interval="15m")` with `middle = SMA(close, period)`, `sigma_pop = sqrt(sum((c - middle)**2) / period)` (population std_dev, divide by `n` not `n-1`, per TradingView convention), `upper = middle + k * sigma_pop`, `lower = middle - k * sigma_pop`. Decimal `.sqrt()` at default 28-digit context preserves precision; tests use 1e-10 tolerance band against irrational sqrt(8). Constructor rejects `period < 2` (degenerate σ) and `std_dev_multiplier <= 0`. `value_json = {"upper", "middle", "lower"}` with Decimal sub-keys; T-110 converts to float at the wire seam. Class docstring documents `value_json` non-hashability per T-106 contract (Mapping/dict instances unhashable). `name_template` includes period + multiplier (e.g. `bollinger_20_2`); multiplier stringified via `format(.normalize(), "f")` so Decimal("2") → "2" (not "2E+0") and Decimal("2.5") → "2.5". `warmup_candles = period`; uses last `period` closes only, regardless of input window length. **`packages/features/builtins/macd.py`** — `MacdFeature(fast=12, slow=26, signal=9, interval="15m")` with standard MACD: macd_line = fast_ema − slow_ema (both SMA-seeded T-107a paradigm); signal_line = SMA-seeded EMA on macd_line series; histogram = macd_line − signal_line. `value_json = {"macd", "signal", "histogram"}` Decimal triple. `warmup_candles = slow + signal − 1 = 34` for default 12/26/9 — operator hand-verified independently before plan submission, plan-reviewer re-verified. Bar-by-bar trace in module docstring: bars 0..25 (26 closes) → first slow_ema at bar 25 (SMA seed); fast_ema series of length 15 (bars 11..25); MACD-line series accumulates over bars 25..33 (9 values total at bar 33 = 34th close, 1-indexed); signal SMA seed of those 9 values → first complete (macd, signal, histogram) triple at bar 33. Constructor rejects `fast < 1`, `slow < 1`, `signal < 1`, and `fast >= slow`. **Module-level helper `_sma_seeded_ema_series(values: Sequence[Decimal], period: int) -> list[Decimal]`** extracted per operator request — returns the EMA value at every bar from index `period - 1` onwards (output length `len(values) - period + 1`). Used by MACD because the per-bar fast/slow alignment requires the SERIES, not just the latest value (single-Decimal helper would force O(n²) iteration). Index-alignment contract documented in helper docstring + inline comment at the slicing site `fast_ema_full[self.slow - self.fast:]` in compute. Helper raises bare `ValueError` (not `FeatureUnderflowError`) on `len(values) < period` — internal-only programmer-error guard, consistent with T-107a constructor `period < 1` raises ValueError pattern. **Golden cross-check test** pins mathematical consistency: `_sma_seeded_ema_series(closes, p)[-1] == EmaFeature(period=p).compute(candles).value_num` — a future change to either's algorithm cannot silently desync MACD's internal EMAs from the public EMA indicator. **Tests** (37 new, ~484 LOC): `test_builtins_vwap.py` (10 cases) covers attributes + 2 weekly/hourly reject cases + underflow + single-bar typical-price + multi-bar same-session hand-computation `(10 + 20 + 30) weighted by (100, 200, 300) → 14000/600` + cross-session UTC-date filter (5 candles spanning 2026-04-25 and 2026-04-26 → result equals VWAP of only Apr-26 session) + zero-volume raises + name_template + protocol; `test_builtins_bollinger.py` (12 cases) covers attributes + period 0/1 reject + std_dev_multiplier 0/-1 reject + custom multiplier 2.5 stringification + underflow + 5-bar period-5 k=2 hand-computation `closes [10,12,14,16,18] → middle=14, variance=8, sigma=√8` (1e-10 tolerance) + constant-prices σ=0 collapse → upper=middle=lower=100 + last-period-window (30 closes, period=5, only last 5 contribute) + name_template + protocol; `test_builtins_macd.py` (15 cases) covers helper underflow + helper output length + helper index alignment + helper period-3 5-value hand-computation `[10,12,14,16,18] → [12,14,16]` + golden cross-check vs EmaFeature for 20-close period-14 + MACD attributes + 3 reject cases (fast/slow/signal=0) + fast >= slow reject + 33-candle underflow + small-MACD hand-computation `fast=2 slow=3 signal=2 warmup=4 closes=[10,12,14,16] → fast=[11,13,15], slow=[12,14], aligned macd_line=[1,1], signal=[1], output {macd:1, signal:1, histogram:0}` + 34-candle warmup boundary returns complete value_json triple + name_template + protocol. Greek σ/α replaced with ASCII `sigma`/`alpha` in docstrings after RUF002 ambiguity warnings. **Cap-relevant LOC**: vwap.py 72 + bollinger.py 77 + macd.py 125 + builtins/__init__.py +6 net = **280 source LOC, under §0.3 cap of 400** (plan estimated ~216; +64 docstring overhead consistent with T-107a precedent ~282 vs ~242 estimate). Tests ~484 (cap-exempt). Coverage 100% on every new module (vwap.py / bollinger.py / macd.py / builtins/__init__.py); protocols.py stays 91% (unchanged from T-106). Verification: ruff/format/mypy(strict) clean (21 features source files, 108 across the workspace), pytest 425 passed + 15 env-gated skipped + 2 warnings in 5.91s (no regressions; baseline 388 from T-107a, +37 net new tests), isolated features suite 92/92 in 1.63s. Plan: docs/plans/T-107b.md (APPROVED 2026-04-26 after one REVISE → fix → re-APPROVE cycle: BLOCKER on VWAP name_template drift from §B.2 verbatim + 2 CONCERNs on helper alignment docstring and value_json non-hashability — all three resolved before re-submission).
- [x] T-107a: 3 scalar built-in indicators (EMA/RSI/ATR) + ADR-0002 pyproject promotion + `FeatureUnderflowError` (2026-04-26) — closes §9.3 line 1488 ("Built-in features live in `packages/features/builtins/`: EMA, SMA, RSI, ATR, Bollinger, VWAP, MACD, OI change, funding rate") for the three scalar Wilder/SMA-seed indicators. T-107b ships VWAP/Bollinger/MACD; SMA/OI change/funding rate deferred to F1+ (no current consumer). §N4 TDD-for-financial-math activates: each indicator written test-first against hand-computable deterministic fixtures with the expected intermediate gains/losses/avg/RS/RSI/ATR documented in test docstrings. **`packages/features/errors.py`** — `FeaturesError(ScalperError)` base + `FeatureUnderflowError(FeaturesError, ValueError)`. Multi-inheritance MRO: `[FeatureUnderflowError, FeaturesError, ScalperError, ValueError, Exception, BaseException, object]` — clean C3 linearisation, mypy-strict-clean (single common ancestor in `Exception`). Primary contract = `FeaturesError` (per §5.4 "Don't raise bare ValueError for domain errors"); `ValueError` inheritance documented as **convenience surface** for callers that already expect `ValueError` for argument-shape violations — the typed family stays the primary catch. **`packages/features/builtins/ema.py`** — `EmaFeature(period, interval="15m")` with TradingView/Wilder seed convention: SMA of first `period` closes, then `EMA_t = α * close_t + (1-α) * EMA_{t-1}` with `α = 2 / (period + 1)`. `warmup_candles = period`. **`packages/features/builtins/rsi.py`** — `RsiFeature(period, interval="15m")` with Wilder smoothing: SMA seed of first `period` gains/losses, then `avg_n = (avg_{n-1} * (period - 1) + current) / period`. `warmup_candles = period + 1` (need `period + 1` closes to produce `period` deltas). Defensive flat-market branch (`avg_loss == 0 AND avg_gain == 0`) returns `Decimal(50)` — neutral midpoint of the 0-100 RSI scale, semantically correct for a "no information" signal. Drift-checker validated as legitimate input class (not §0.8 anti-hypothetical), covered by `test_no_movement_returns_50`. **`packages/features/builtins/atr.py`** — `AtrFeature(period, interval="15m")` with Wilder smoothing: SMA seed of first `period` true ranges, where `TR_i = max(high_i - low_i, |high_i - close_{i-1}|, |low_i - close_{i-1}|)`. `warmup_candles = period + 1`. **All three indicators are regular classes** (not frozen dataclasses) per `OhlcBackfill`/`OhlcPipeline` precedent — convention crystallised: frozen+slotted dataclass = immutable value type; regular class = stateful service object. Indicators carry `period`/`interval`/`name_template`/`source_version`/`warmup_candles` as instance attributes set in `__init__`. **Stateless `compute`** — re-processes the entire window from scratch each call. Engine (T-110) holds the rolling buffer; indicators do not cache prior state on the instance. O(N) per indicator per closed candle (N = warmup_candles + small) is negligible CPU at sub-10-bot scale. **`name_template` instance-baked** — `f"ind.{{symbol}}.{{interval}}.<algo>_{period}"` substitutes `{period}` at construction time, leaving only `{symbol}`/`{interval}` for the T-111 registry layer. **Decimal end-to-end** — preserves §7.2 NUMERIC(30,12) precision through compute; T-110 will convert to `float` at the §8.4 wire seam. Default 28-digit Decimal context; no global mutator (§N6). **Underflow → `FeatureUnderflowError`** with explicit message naming the indicator + `period` + minimum candle count + actual count, e.g. `"EMA(period=20) requires >= 20 candles, got 19"`. The engine MUST respect the warmup contract; violation = bug, fail loud per §0.4. **`packages/features/pyproject.toml`** promoted from 5-line virtual stub to full hatch scaffold per ADR-0002 surprise 1 (first multi-component subpackage `builtins/` is exactly the trigger). Verbatim mirror of `packages/db/pyproject.toml` with `dev-mode-dirs = ["."]` retained, sources remap `"" = "packages/features"`, dependencies = `["scalper-v2-core"]`, `[tool.uv.sources] scalper-v2-core = { workspace = true }`. Description updated to reflect target six-indicator scope (T-107b ships the rest in the same phase). `uv.lock` regenerated — `scalper-v2-features` becomes editable-installed across the workspace; no spurious dependency churn. **Tests** (38 new, ~480 LOC): `test_errors.py` (7 cases) covers MRO subclass invariants + str message round-trip + no-arg constructor; `test_builtins_ema.py` (10 cases) covers attribute set per period + period-zero/negative reject + custom interval + underflow + 5-bar EMA(3) hand-computation `[10,12,14,16,18] → SMA seed 12, alpha 0.5, EMA = 16` + warmup-boundary returns SMA seed + Decimal precision at NUMERIC(30,12) floor + name_template substitution + Feature protocol typecheck; `test_builtins_rsi.py` (11 cases) covers attributes + period-zero reject + custom interval + underflow at 14 closes (need ≥15) + 15-close synthetic Wilder fixture with hand-computed `avg_gain=3.34/14, avg_loss=1.40/14, RS=2.385714, RSI=70.46413502109704` (±1e-10 tolerance) + 4-close period-2 one-Wilder-step fixture `[10,12,11,13] → RS=6, RSI=600/7=85.71428...` + all-gains → RSI=100 + all-losses → RSI=0 + flat-market dual-zero → RSI=50 (defensive branch covered) + name_template + protocol; `test_builtins_atr.py` (9 cases) covers attributes + period-zero reject + custom interval + underflow + 5-bar ATR(2) hand-computation `TRs=[3,4,2,3] → SMA seed 3.5, Wilder steps → 2.875` + gap-up TR-dominance (`|high - prev_close|` > `high - low`) + gap-down TR-dominance (`|low - prev_close|` > `high - low`) + name_template + protocol. Test fixture choice: synthetic-with-hand-computed-expected-values rather than canonical Wilder 1978 book fixture (book not in repo, copyright); the synthetic 15-close sequence is reproducible and auditable in PR diff. **Cap-relevant LOC**: errors.py 39 + builtins/__init__.py 20 + builtins/ema.py 55 + builtins/rsi.py 78 + builtins/atr.py 68 + features/__init__.py +8 net + pyproject.toml +27 net = **295 source LOC, under §0.3 cap of 400**. Tests ~480 (cap-exempt). Coverage 100% on every new module (errors.py / ema.py / rsi.py / atr.py / builtins/__init__.py). protocols.py stays 91% (unchanged — ellipsis body of `compute`). Verification: ruff/format/mypy(strict) clean (15 features source files, 102 across the workspace), pytest 388 passed + 15 env-gated skipped + 2 warnings in 5.55s, isolated features suite 55/55 in 1.58s. Hazards addressed: §N4 (TDD-for-financial-math activated). No §20 hazards directly addressed by indicator math itself.
- [x] T-106: `packages/features` skeleton + `Feature` protocol + `FeatureValue` types (2026-04-26) — closes §9.3 r. 1500-1509 by landing the typing contract that T-107 (6 built-in indicators) and T-110 feature-engine will compute against. Pure typing scaffold — no compute logic, no I/O. **`packages/features/types.py`** ships two frozen+slotted dataclasses: `OhlcCandle` (domain candle: symbol, interval, bucket_start, OHLC, volume, source — Decimal across the board to preserve §7.2 `NUMERIC(30, 12)` precision through compute; no `is_closed` field because only closed candles cross the T-110 wire→domain seam) and `FeatureValue` (lean shape: exactly one of `value_num: Decimal | None` / `value_bool: bool | None` / `value_json: Mapping[str, object] | None` is non-None, enforced via `__post_init__`). Metadata (feature_name, symbol, computed_at, source_version) is intentionally **not** carried on `FeatureValue` — `Feature.compute` is a pure compute kernel that doesn't know its own registered name; feature-engine and scoring layers hold metadata alongside the value as needed. **`packages/features/protocols.py`** ships `Feature` Protocol (4 attributes — `name_template`/`source_version`/`interval`/`warmup_candles` — plus sync `compute(candles: Sequence[OhlcCandle]) -> FeatureValue`). **No `@runtime_checkable`** per operator decision: `runtime_checkable` only checks methods, not data attributes, so `isinstance(obj, Feature)` would silently accept implementations missing `name_template`/`interval`/etc. — false sense of security. T-111 plugin discovery does explicit attribute introspection if needed. **`compute` is sync** because it is pure CPU over a `warmup_candles`-bounded window — §5.5 mandates async only for I/O. **5 operator decisions baked into the plan** (`docs/plans/T-106.md`): (1) `value_num=Decimal` preserves NUMERIC(30,12) through compute; T-110 converts to `float` at the §8.4 `FeatureUpdate` publish seam; (2) `OhlcCandle` is a fresh dataclass in `packages/features/types.py` (not reused from `packages.bus.schemas.OhlcCandlePayload` Pydantic or `packages.market.rest.OhlcCandle`) — keeps `packages.features` decoupled from bus and market closures; T-110 maps wire payload → domain candle at the seam (~10 LOC mapping fn there, out of T-106 scope); (3) no `@runtime_checkable`; (4) `value_json: Mapping[str, object]` (read-only abstraction; typed union would prematurely fix the schema — Bollinger upper/middle/lower vs MACD signal/histogram have different shapes); (5) `pyproject.toml` stays virtual stub per ADR-0002 (no `[build-system]`) — no external runtime deps, no other workspace member depends on `scalper-v2-features` yet. Promotion deferred to T-107 (subpackage `builtins/` triggers ADR-0002 surprise 1) or T-110 (first service workspace dep). `pyproject.toml` description string tightened from "Scaffold stub; implementation lands in F1." to reflect T-106 content. **Hashability scope** (plan-reviewer write-time hook): `value_num` and `value_bool` variants are hashable (Decimal and bool both are); `value_json` variant is **not** hashable because `Mapping` instances (typically `dict`) are unhashable — documented behaviour, not a defect. Three positive-path tests cover both hashable variants + a `test_value_json_variant_is_unhashable` documenting the expected `TypeError`. **Tests** (18 new, ~167 test LOC): `test_types.py` (15 cases) covers OhlcCandle frozen + slotted (`__slots__` introspection — frozen+slots dataclasses raise `FrozenInstanceError` on any attribute assignment, so the slot test asserts `__slots__` presence rather than hitting AttributeError on unknown attrs), Decimal precision round-trip at NUMERIC(30,12) precision floor (`Decimal("50000.123456789012")` matching T-104a fixture pattern), value-by-value equality, FeatureValue construction for each of the three variants, all four invalid combinations (zero/two/three non-None) raise `ValueError`, frozen, hashability scope. `test_protocols.py` (3 cases) covers a toy `_AlwaysOneFeature` impl satisfying the Protocol via direct annotation (`feature: Feature = _AlwaysOneFeature()` typechecks under mypy strict), `compute([])` returns expected `FeatureValue(value_num=Decimal("1"))`, and attribute access for the four required Protocol attrs. Cap-relevant LOC: types.py 103 + protocols.py 59 + __init__.py 15 + tests 167 + plan 155 + pyproject.toml description delta = ~500 insertions total; ~177 cap-relevant source under §0.3 cap of 400 (overhead is load-bearing docstring rationale per write-time hooks, not implementation). Coverage: types.py 100% / __init__.py 100% / protocols.py 91% (one branch miss is the Protocol method `...` body, non-executable by design — same pattern as T-104b ohlc.py 98%). Verification: ruff/format/mypy(strict) clean (6 features-package source files, 102 across the workspace), pytest 351 passed + 15 env-gated skipped + 2 warnings in 5.53s, isolated features suite 18/18 in 1.38s. Hazards addressed: none directly — pure typing scaffold. H-007/H-014 are upstream (T-101b/T-102/T-105); §N4 TDD-for-financial-math activates at T-107 with concrete EMA/RSI/etc. compute logic.
- [x] T-105: backfill on startup + reconnect resync via Binance REST `/api/v3/klines` (2026-04-26) — closes §9.2 lines 1464-1471 by plugging the gap between the most recent `ohlc_1m` row (or a 24h cold-start window) and `now` on every successful WS connect — initial + each reconnect — so frames missed during disconnects get repaired. Idempotency rides on T-104a's `insert_ohlc_1m` `ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE`; backfill adds no new external write. **`packages/market/backfill.py`** — `OhlcBackfill` thin coordinator (DI'd `rest`/`pool`/`logger`/`initial_hours`/`per_symbol_pause_seconds`), public `async run_for_symbols(symbols)` method. Per-symbol seriality with a 50 ms inter-symbol `asyncio.sleep` (rate-limit-friendly at sub-10-bot scale, avoids hammering Binance when many symbols all reconnect at once). Page-loop against `/api/v3/klines` (`limit=1000` per page, Binance maximum); cursor advances by `candles[-1].bucket_start + 1m`; empty REST page breaks the loop (no infinite retry). End-time floor `now.replace(s=0, us=0) - 1m` skips the in-progress minute (the WS path delivers it as the `x=true` closed-bucket frame at the next tick — without this floor, REST would yield an under-reported "closed" candle for the un-closed current minute and pollute `ohlc_1m`). Per-symbol `try/except Exception` (NOT bare except, so `CancelledError` propagates and shutdown isn't masked) → log `ohlc_backfill_symbol_error` + skip; remaining symbols still run. **`BinanceWsClient` extension** — single optional `on_connect: Callable[[], Awaitable[None]] | None = None` kwarg on `__init__`; `await self._on_connect()` runs after each successful connect (initial + every reconnect) and after the SUBSCRIBE frame, before the receive loop blocks on `__anext__`. The composition root wires it as `lambda: asyncio.create_task(backfill.run_for_symbols(settings.symbols))` — fire-and-forget so the WS receive loop never stalls on a long REST page-loop. Two concurrent backfill tasks (e.g. fast reconnect during a running fill) are safe because `insert_ohlc_1m` is idempotent on `(symbol, bucket_start, source)` PK; no in-flight lock per the operator decision (premature complexity at H-007 backoff frequencies). **`fetch_latest_ohlc_bucket(conn, *, symbol, source) -> datetime | None`** — read-only anchor query, no `@idempotent`/`@non_idempotent` marker (markers are for external writes per §N3). Returns `max(bucket_start)` for `(symbol, source)`, or `None` on cold-start so the caller falls back to the configurable initial-hours window. **Settings extension** (`services/market_data/app/config.py`): `binance_rest_url: str = "https://api.binance.com"` and `backfill_initial_hours: int = 24` — operator-decided 24h cold-start default seeds caggs with enough history to verify the F1 exit criterion on a fresh deploy; subsequent restarts use `last_bucket+1m` once `ohlc_1m` has rows. T-100's explicit "BINANCE_REST_URL out-of-scope for T-100" docstring lifted now that T-105 is the in-scope task. **Composition root extension** (`services/market_data/app/main.py`): in lifespan, `rest = BinanceRestClient(...)` + `backfill = OhlcBackfill(...)` constructed before `ws` so the `on_connect` callback can close over `backfill`; `app.state.rest` and `app.state.backfill` attached. Shutdown order extends to `pipeline.stop → ws.close → ws_task await → bus.close → rest.close → pool.close` — `rest.close()` (httpx pool drain) runs after `bus.close()` and before `pool.close()` so in-flight backfill tasks resolve their last REST call against the still-open asyncpg pool. Lifespan + shutdown docstrings (load-bearing operational invariants per T-100 precedent) renumbered to reflect the 15-step lifecycle. **Tests** (15 unit + 2 ws + 3 integration = 20 new tests, ~700 LOC): `tests/test_backfill.py` covers cold-start (no rows → start_time = end - 24h, 1440 candles across 2 pages), gap-fill (last_bucket exists → start = last + 1m), no-gap short-circuit, empty REST page breaks loop, page boundary cursor advance, `end_time` excludes in-progress minute, REST error per-symbol isolation, persist error per-symbol isolation (mid-run `_FakeConn.execute` patch via `unittest.mock.patch`), multi-symbol seriality + n-1 inter-symbol sleeps via patched `asyncio.sleep`, `per_symbol_pause_seconds=0` short-circuit, Decimal precision round-trip at NUMERIC(30,12) precision floor, `CancelledError` mid-loop propagates through `except Exception` (not absorbed), empty `symbols=[]` no-op, default-constructor wiring against a `MagicMock`+`AsyncMock` REST. `tests/test_ws.py` extends with `test_on_connect_callback_fires_on_initial_and_each_reconnect` (3 successful connects × 2 outages → callback called 3x) and `test_on_connect_default_none_does_not_raise` (backward-compat). `tests/integration/queries/test_market_data.py` extends with `fetch_latest_ohlc_bucket` returns None on empty / max(bucket_start) / source filter isolates binance vs bybit. `services/market_data/tests/conftest.py` + `test_app_factory.py` extended with `mock_rest` fixture + `BinanceRestClient` patched at the import boundary so existing T-100 lifespan tests still pass; `app.state.rest` + `app.state.backfill` asserted post-startup. **Cap-relevant LOC**: `backfill.py` 210 + queries/market_data.py +27 + market `__init__` +5 + ws.py +13 + config.py +9 + main.py +80 net = **344, under §0.3 cap of 400**. Most of the main.py expansion is docstring (lifespan order renumbered + on_connect contract + backfill section); load-bearing per T-100 precedent. Verification: ruff/format/mypy(strict) clean (101 source files), pytest 333 passed + 15 env-gated skipped + 2 warnings in 5.26s, backfill.py coverage 100%. Hazards addressed: H-007 (on_connect kwarg is additive; existing exp-backoff test unchanged + two new on_connect tests).
- [x] T-100: market-data-svc skeleton — FastAPI + lifespan composition root (2026-04-25) — wires the F1 market-data path: asyncpg pool + `NatsClient` + `BinanceWsClient` (T-101b) + `SubscriptionManager` (T-102) + `OhlcPipeline` (T-104b) via the FastAPI lifespan. Spec: §9.2 service def, §19 F1 bullet 2 endpoint set, §18.1/§18.4 compose+healthcheck, ADR-0002 hatch scaffold. **Composition root** in `services/market_data/app/main.py` uses a **forwarding-closure holder pattern** to resolve the `BinanceWsClient` ↔ `SubscriptionManager` construction-time circular dependency: ws is built with a closure handler reading from a single-element list (`dispatch_holder: list[SubscriptionManager]` local to lifespan scope per §N6), manager is built referencing ws, manager is appended to the holder so the closure resolves to `manager.dispatch`. Microsecond pre-bind window between ws construction and holder append is documented in module doc lines 81-93; warning log `market_data_dispatch_pre_bind` surfaces any future regression that breaks the synchronous ordering invariant — explicit warning to future readers not to "tighten" by adding a lock-until-manager-bound. **Race note for steps 7→8** (module doc lines 56-65): `pipeline.start()` may run before ws CONNECTED — per T-101b contract, `ws.add_stream()` is safe in any state and defers SUBSCRIBE to next reconnect cycle, so no `ws.wait_connected()` needed. **Lifespan order** (load-bearing): pool → bus.connect → ws (with closure handler) → manager → holder.append → pipeline → state attach → `asyncio.create_task(ws.run())` → `pipeline.start(symbols)`. Shutdown reverse: `pipeline.stop` → `ws.close` → ws_task await with 5s `asyncio.timeout` (defensive cancel + `contextlib.suppress(CancelledError)` on timeout, log `ws_task_shutdown_timeout`) → `bus.close` → `pool.close`. Reverse order is load-bearing: `pipeline.stop` must run before `ws.close` so per-symbol task `__aexit__` UNSUBSCRIBE frames land while WS is still open. **`/ready` three-check** (`services/market_data/app/health.py`) — bus.state == CONNECTED, then pool.acquire(timeout=1s), then ws.state == CONNECTED. Reasons bus → db → ws on first failure (cheapest-check-first ordering; precedence asserted by tests). RECONNECTING → 503 `reason="ws"` is the deliberate F1 contract (operator visibility into outages beats grace-period heuristics that mask real Binance downtime); F1+ entry queued for grace-period semantics if LB/k8s restart loops surface during transient Binance outages. **Symbol-seed deviation** (§9.2 line 1454 specifies `bots` JOIN `bot_configs` query but F3's bot registry hasn't shipped): `MARKET_DATA_SYMBOLS` env-var stopgap with `Settings.symbols` property handling empty-string + repeated-separator + whitespace cases via `[s.strip() for s in split(",") if s.strip()]` (8-param parametrize coverage). Empty default → empty list → `OhlcPipeline.start([])` no-op → service stays healthy + ready. Documented as §6.7 procedural deviation in module doc; no ADR per operator decision (would be one-paragraph stub without architectural debate weight; F1+ entry queued for the mechanical swap when F3 lands). **No backfill in T-100** — T-105 (queued, top-of-DAG now) ships REST `/api/v3/klines` startup + reconnect resync; T-100 starts pipeline cold and the first closed-bucket arrives ≤60s after WS connect. **Settings** (`config.py`) mirrors signal-gateway pattern (pydantic-settings + `extra="ignore"`): service_name, log_level (Literal), http_port=8000 (compose service-name DNS isolates from signal-gateway:8000), nats_url, database_url (required), market_data_symbols. Explicitly NOT included per §0.8: `BINANCE_WS_URL`, `BINANCE_REST_URL`, HMAC secrets — out-of-scope for T-100. **DI providers** in `deps.py` (7 providers: pool/bus/ws/subscription_mgr/pipeline/settings/logger) — all read from `request.app.state` with `typing.cast` for mypy. **Dockerfile** two-stage mirror of signal-gateway: same base image (python:3.12.13-slim-trixie), same uv-CLI donor (ghcr.io/astral-sh/uv:0.11.7), same `--package scalper-v2-market-data --frozen --no-dev` install, distinct UID/GID 10002 for `market` user (vs signal-gateway's 10001) for per-service log attribution if F1+ adds host bind mount. **compose.yaml** entry mirrors signal-gateway block: same env_file `secrets.env required: false` pattern, same `depends_on` (postgres healthy + nats healthy + nats-init completed), same healthcheck (`python -c urllib.request` against `/health`); `MARKET_DATA_SYMBOLS: ""` env-stopgap with operator-override docstring; no nginx route (internal-only, no public surface). **Prometheus scrape entry** in `infra/prometheus/prometheus.yml` mirrors signal-gateway's job def. **Tests** (29 tests, 555 LOC): `test_config.py` (4 tests + 8-param symbols-split parametrize covering `""`/`"BTCUSDT"`/`"BTCUSDT,ETHUSDT"`/`"BTCUSDT,,ETHUSDT"`/`",BTCUSDT,"`/`"  BTCUSDT  , ETHUSDT "`/`",,,"`/`"   "`); `test_health.py` (1 test); `test_ready.py` (9 tests — happy + 6 fail-reason cases for bus/db/ws + 2 precedence cases proving bus → db → ws cheapest-first ordering); `test_app_factory.py` (7 tests — factory shape, route registration, /metrics serves default collectors, sync state attach pre-lifespan, async state attach post-lifespan, MARKET_DATA_SYMBOLS → Settings.symbols → OhlcPipeline.start passthrough with `["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT"]` and empty `[]` cases). `conftest.py` mocks asyncpg pool / NatsClient / BinanceWsClient at the import boundary so the real lifespan exercises end-to-end against fakes; `_FakeWs` `run()` blocks on never-set asyncio.Event mirroring T-101b's "wait until close" loop shape. Helper `_build_app_with_pipeline_capture` extracts the OhlcPipeline-mocked variant so symbols-passthrough tests stay terse (~5 lines per test). `pytest` import noqa-TC002'd in `test_app_factory.py` because pytest fixture resolution introspects type hints at runtime — moving under TYPE_CHECKING would break `monkeypatch: pytest.MonkeyPatch` resolution. **Cap-relevant LOC**: Python source 548 + infra (Dockerfile + compose + prometheus delta) 146 = **694, OVER §0.3 cap of 400**. Accepted per operator decision: main.py docstrings are load-bearing (composition order walkthrough + holder-pattern rationale + race-note + symbol-seed deviation + no-backfill cross-ref encode operational invariants future readers need to maintain the lifespan); §0.3 cap is anti-complexity-creep, not anti-essential-documentation. Dockerfile + compose + prometheus deltas qualify under §0.3 generated-artifacts exception per T-015a precedent. Splitting into T-100a/T-100b creates an arbitrary seam without LOC benefit (T-100b would still be over-cap). - [x] T-104b: `OhlcPipeline` consumer + per-symbol task lifecycle (2026-04-25) — second half of the original T-104 (split from T-104a's pre-flagged contingency triggered by 553-LOC over-cap mid-Write); consumes T-104a's `OhlcCandlePayload` schema + `insert_ohlc_1m` query. Spec: §9.2 OHLC pipeline, §8.2 MARKET_OHLC stream config, §8.4 OHLCCandle payload. **`packages/market/ohlc.py`** ships `OhlcPipeline` — composed by the market-data-svc composition root (T-100, future) with `subscription_mgr` + `pool` + `bus` + `logger` DI'd, no I/O resources owned directly. Lifecycle: `start(symbols)` spawns one `asyncio.create_task` per symbol (each task running `async with subscription_mgr.subscribe(symbol) as feed: async for frame in feed: await self._handle(symbol, frame)`); `stop()` cancels all tasks and awaits them via `asyncio.timeout(stop_timeout_seconds=5.0)` + `asyncio.gather(return_exceptions=True)`. Per-task SubscriptionManager release on context exit decrements refcounts; if no other consumer holds the symbol, the underlying WS streams are torn down (T-102 H-014). **Per-frame classification** by `data.k.x` boolean (Binance kline canonical closed-bucket flag, true on the terminal frame of a minute bucket and false on every prior intra-minute update): `True` → `_persist_then_publish` (`insert_ohlc_1m` via `pool.acquire()`, then `bus.publish` of `market.ohlc.1m.<symbol>` envelope with deterministic uuid5 `Nats-Msg-Id` from `message_id_for_closed_candle`); `False` → `_publish_in_progress` (no DB write, fresh `uuid4` envelope per call so every intra-bucket tick is its own message — server-side dedup would lose intermediate ticks); missing/non-bool `x` or non-kline `e` event or non-dict `k` or missing `data` → log `ohlc_pipeline_malformed_frame` + drop. **Publish-after-persist ordering** with explicit downstream-consumer contract documented in module doc lines 32-46: T-110 feature-engine and any other consumer of `market.ohlc.>` MUST treat the DB as canonical source-of-truth and the NATS stream as a live tap (warmup reads from `ohlc_*` continuous aggregates at startup; bus is low-latency notification only). Persist failure → no publish + log `ohlc_pipeline_persist_error`. Publish failure after persist → DB row stands + log `ohlc_pipeline_publish_error`; downstream recovers via DB read at next warmup. The opposite order (publish-before-persist) would let a phantom candle leak onto the bus that does not exist in DB — backfill cannot repair because the canonical source-of-truth is the DB itself. **Stateless closed-detection** (no per-symbol `last_closed` dict, no in-memory dedup): idempotency rides on the DB PK (T-104a's `ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE`) plus the deterministic uuid5 `Nats-Msg-Id`. Module doc + `_handle` docstring both warn future readers off adding a cache (would be restart-unsafe and race-prone; T-105 backfill is the recovery path for any frames missed during a disconnect). **Per-symbol task error semantics**: handler raises → log `ohlc_pipeline_handler_error` + continue with the next frame (task stays alive); `except Exception` (NOT bare `except`) so `asyncio.CancelledError` propagates through to the `async with` exit and `stop()` can shut the consumer down promptly — explicit comment placed at the per-frame except site so a future "tighten error handling" pass doesn't broaden the catch. No auto-restart in F1 (operator restarts the service). **Symbol set source-of-truth**: callers pass `symbols: list[str]` to `start()`; the pipeline does NOT query DB for the active-symbol JOIN — that lives with the composition root (T-100 lifespan, future), keeping the pipeline pure-class testable. **Subject + correlation_id construction**: `market.ohlc.1m.<symbol>` and `f"ohlc:{symbol}:{bucket_start.isoformat()}"` (typed as `CorrelationId` newtype). `tests/test_ohlc.py` (25 tests, 584 LOC) covers frame classification (closed/in-progress/missing-x/non-bool-x/non-kline-event/missing-data/non-dict-k), publish-after-persist ordering (persist-fail-skips-publish, publish-fail-after-persist-keeps-row, in-progress-publish-fail-no-DB-write), 3-in-progress-then-closed multi-frame sequence with correct `is_closed` flag ordering, out-of-order closed (DB ON CONFLICT contract handles repair, pipeline issues INSERT regardless), Decimal precision flow at NUMERIC(30,12) precision floor (`50000.123456789012` round-trips intact), deterministic uuid5 on closed publishes (matches `message_id_for_closed_candle` exactly) + distinct uuid4 per in-progress tick, subject `market.ohlc.1m.<symbol>` for ETHUSDT route, correlation_id `ohlc:BTCUSDT:2024-04-25T12:00:00+00:00`, start/stop lifecycle (idempotent start, no-op stop-before-start, empty-symbols spawns no tasks, stop cancels cleanly within timeout), per-symbol task isolation (handler error on A doesn't kill B; both publish independently), CancelledError propagation (`stop()` exits within 0.5s on parked consumer — proves `except Exception` not bare), and direct `_consume_symbol` coverage (bad-frame-then-good-frame in the same feed proves per-frame except keeps iteration alive). `_FakeSubMgr`/`_FakeFeed`/`_FakePool`/`_FakeBus` test stubs mirror only the methods OhlcPipeline touches. `MessageEnvelope` kept as runtime import (used as runtime annotation on `_FakeBus.publish` parameter and `_FakeBus.publish_calls` list type — `# noqa: TC001` with rationale comment); pure annotation-only types stay under `TYPE_CHECKING` per project convention. Cap-relevant LOC delta: ohlc.py 335 + __init__.py +4 = 339 (under §0.3 cap of 400, exactly matching the T-104a split-time projection). Coverage on ohlc.py: 98% (uncovered lines 164-165 are the `except TimeoutError` warning log in `stop()` — reliable wedge fixtures fight Python 3.11+ `asyncio.Task` cancel-state semantics where every `await` checkpoint raises CancelledError once `task.cancel()` is called; `task.uncancel()` in a loop still resolves before the 200 ms test budget. The log path remains in production code as the real safety-net for a wedged consumer; not fabricated synthetically per §0.8 — explicit code comment placed at the dropped-test site explains the deliberate gap). Verification: ruff/format/mypy clean (13 source files in `packages/market`, 90 across the workspace), pytest 25/25 in 1.81s for the new file (89/89 across `packages/market`), 287 passed + 12 skipped in 4.65s project-wide (no regressions). Both jobs green at `70a6202`: ci-fast #62 26s, ci-full #28 1m 13s.

ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE` on PK `(symbol, bucket_start, source)`. **DO UPDATE not DO NOTHING** rationale: T-105 backfill via REST `/api/v3/klines` is the canonical truth source, so a WS-stored row corrupted by a future bug must be repairable; closed-bucket Binance frames are deterministic so the typical re-write is a no-op against identical values (one WAL record/min/symbol — negligible at scale). Genuinely idempotent (same inputs → same row state) — no `@non_idempotent` marker, differs from `insert_signal` which returns a fresh `id` per call. Caller (T-104b `OhlcPipeline`) wraps in try/except so transient PG errors are logged + dropped rather than killing the per-symbol consumer task; T-105 fills any gap. No regression in existing `tests/grafana`, `tests/integration/migrations`, or `services/signal_gateway/tests/integration` trees (all 12 env-gated skips fire correctly post-fix). `packages/bus/tests/test_market_ohlc_schema.py` (15 unit tests, 213 LOC) covers field defaults / pinned-Literal rejection (`interval="5m"` / `source="bybit"` / `schema_version="2.0"` all raise) / UTC enforcement on `bucket_start` (naive rejected, CEST rejected, zero-offset aware normalised to `datetime.UTC`) / frozen / Decimal precision JSON round-trip at 12 fractional digits / `+00:00` wire form (not bare `Z`) / `message_id_for_closed_candle` determinism + UUID v5 + cross-helper namespace isolation against `signals.message_id_for` (guards against accidental shared NS in a future refactor) + UTC contract on the helper input. `tests/integration/queries/test_market_data.py` (8 integration tests, 229 LOC, env-gated `POSTGRES_TEST_DSN`) covers single-row INSERT with `NUMERIC(30, 12)` precision survival, ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE last-write-wins value-level assertion (catches a regression to DO NOTHING), identical-values re-insert no-op behaviour, and distinct PK tuples — symbol/bucket_start/source — each create independent rows. - [x] T-102: `SubscriptionManager` refcount + H-014 hazard test (2026-04-25) — `packages/market/subscription.py` ships `SubscriptionManager` (refcounted facade over `BinanceWsClient` per H-014), `SymbolFeed` (per-subscriber async iterator over Binance multiplex frames), and the private `_Subscription` async-CM. Public API: `async with mgr.subscribe("BTCUSDT") as feed: async for frame in feed: ...` — 0→1 transition issues `add_stream` for the §9.2 line 1455 pair (`btcusdt@kline_1m` + `btcusdt@bookTicker`) on the underlying `BinanceWsClient`; 1→0 issues `remove_stream` for both kinds and signals `StopAsyncIteration` on the surviving feed. Per-symbol counter under a single `asyncio.Lock` (one lock per manager — fewer locks, lower contention at sub-10-bot scale beats per-symbol granularity). Lock held across `dispatch` enqueue (sync `put_nowait`, no `await` under the lock) so a concurrent release cannot leak a real frame past EOF in the survivor's queue. Symbol shape validated synchronously at `subscribe()` call site (uppercase ASCII alphanumeric — rejects `btcusdt`, `BTC.P`, `BTC USDT`, non-ASCII; accepts `BTCUSDT`, `1INCHUSDT`, `1000PEPEUSDT`); fail-fast at the call site instead of producing a malformed Binance stream name that Binance silently ignores. **Queue policy** (single-module decision, no ADR per §0.6 — sensible default + escape hatch via `feed_maxsize` constructor arg): bounded `asyncio.Queue` per feed (default `maxsize=1024`), drop-oldest on overflow, optional `subscription_feed_overflow_total{symbol}` counter (Prometheus Counter, injected by composition root) + `subscription_feed_overflow` warning log. T-104 (OHLC pipeline) treats the contract as "may drop intermediate frames under back-pressure"; closed-bucket detection rides on the next in-progress frame's monotonic `bucket_start` regardless. **Reconnect interaction**: during a WS outage `BinanceWsClient` is RECONNECTING and dispatches no frames; feeds silently block on `__anext__` until reconnect resumes traffic — no spurious EOF, no exception. Documented "feed silence ≠ unsubscribed" so callers needing liveness pair the `async for` with `asyncio.timeout`. **Symbol resolution boundary**: SubscriptionManager takes canonical symbols (`BTCUSDT`) and translates to Binance stream names internally; T-008/T-010 `symbol_map` does NOT touch this layer — that translation lives upstream in signal-gateway (TradingView aliases → canonical Bybit). Lifecycle: SubscriptionManager is **injected** with a `BinanceWsClient` instance (N6 — no globals, DI via constructors); the service composition root (T-100 `market-data-svc.main.py` lifespan) creates the WS client, creates SubscriptionManager bound to it, wires `manager.dispatch` as the WS handler, then runs `asyncio.create_task(ws.run())` independently. `tests/test_subscription_manager.py` (32 tests, 477 LOC) covers symbol-shape validation (6 reject + 4 accept params), refcount transitions (0→1, 1→2, 2→1, 1→0, distinct-symbol independence), **H-014 hazard test** `test_refcount_sub_survives_one_caller_releasing` (verbatim §20 name) — two callers acquire `BTCUSDT`, A releases, asserts (a) `ws.streams` still contains both stream names, (b) `ws.remove_calls == []`, (c) released feed yields `StopAsyncIteration`, (d) survivor receives subsequently-dispatched frame, (e) final 1→0 fires on survivor's exit; dispatch fan-out + cross-symbol isolation + ack-frame ignore (4-param `{"result": null, "id": N}` / non-`@` stream / missing stream / non-string stream); kline+bookTicker pair both land in feed; `stream_kinds` constructor override reduces pair to singleton; 10-way concurrent `asyncio.gather` `__aenter__` issues exactly one `add_stream` per kind; release-during-dispatch lock-serialisation race; EOF on parked `__anext__` consumer + clean `async for` exit; overflow drop-oldest preserves freshest frame + counter increment with `{"symbol": "BTCUSDT"}` label; `overflow_counter=None` no-op path; structural smoke that `BinanceWsClient` still exposes `add_stream`/`remove_stream` (T-101b/T-102 seam tripwire). `_FakeWsClient` test stub mirrors only the methods SubscriptionManager touches (`add_stream`/`remove_stream`/`streams`); `# type: ignore[arg-type]` at construction (structural compat without nominal subclassing — same pattern T-101b uses for `_FakeWs` vs `ClientConnection`). Operator design-review flags resolved during write: (a) double-exit test dropped per §0.8 (no concrete `async with` path triggers `__aexit__` twice); (b) symbol shape validation added as one-predicate-line; (c) EOF-via-`StopAsyncIteration` contract documented in `SymbolFeed` docstring so callers don't catch `BinanceWsError` expecting feed end. Cap-relevant LOC delta: subscription.py 299 + __init__.py +6 = 305 (under §0.3 cap of 400, despite docstring-heavy module covering H-014 contract + queue policy + reconnect interaction + symbol vocabulary). Coverage on subscription.py: 92% (uncovered branches are the EOF-on-full-queue overflow recovery in `_signal_eof` and the `_release` early-return on count==0 double-release path — defensive, not anti-hypothetically fabricated per §0.8). - [x] T-101b: Binance WS client + H-007 reconnect (2026-04-25) — `packages/market/ws.py` ships `BinanceWsClient` (long-lived public-market-data WS connection driving a caller-supplied async handler per JSON frame) + `ConnectionState` enum (DISCONNECTED → CONNECTING → CONNECTED ⇄ RECONNECTING → CLOSED), packaged with the H-007 reconnect contract: exponential backoff 1s→60s with full jitter via `exp_backoff_delays` from T-101a; the loop re-subscribes the current stream set on every successful reconnect; long-disconnect signal (structured `binance_ws_long_disconnect` log + `long_disconnect_count` counter) increments once per outage when elapsed disconnect time crosses the configurable 60s threshold and resets on successful reconnect so a later outage can fire again. `add_stream`/`remove_stream` optimistically mutate the internal stream set: SUBSCRIBE/UNSUBSCRIBE frame sent inline when CONNECTED, otherwise the change takes effect on the next reconnect; idempotent on duplicates/unknowns; no ack tracking (Binance's `{result: null, id: N}` is informational, subscription liveness observable via incoming data).
